# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

The file includes **42 C++ source files** organized across three main areas:

### **1. Frame Construction (layout/base/)**
- `nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h` - Frame tree construction from DOM
- `nsFrameManager.cpp/h` - Frame tree management

### **2. Block Layout Reflow (layout/generic/)**
- `nsBlockFrame.cpp/h` - Core block layout implementation
- `BlockReflowState.cpp/h` - Block reflow state management
- `nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h` - Block child reflow context
- `ReflowInput.cpp/h` - Reflow input parameters
- `ReflowOutput.cpp/h` - Reflow output metrics
- `nsLineLayout.cpp/h` - Inline line layout
- `nsLineBox.cpp/h` - Line box management
- `nsFloatManager.cpp/h` - Float positioning
- `AbsoluteContainingBlock.cpp/h` - Absolute/fixed positioning

### **3. Dirty Frame Invalidation (layout/generic/)**
- `nsFrameStateBits.h` - Frame state bit definitions
- `nsFrameState.cpp/h` - Frame state management
- `nsIFrame.cpp/h` - Frame interface with dirty bit methods
- Supporting classes for marking/clearing dirty frames

### **4. Reflow Orchestration (layout/base/)**
- `PresShell.cpp/h` - Main reflow entry point
- `nsPresContext.cpp/h` - Presentation context
- `nsRefreshDriver.cpp/h` - Reflow scheduling & timing
- `nsIReflowCallback.h` - Reflow callback interface

The answer includes a detailed narrative explaining how these components work together to implement incremental layout updates through the reflow pipeline.

layout engine reflow pipeline in Mozilla Firefox (gecko-dev) comprises three interconnected subsystems:\\n\\n**1. FRAME CONSTRUCTION PHASE (layout/base/)**\\nThe frame construction subsystem, implemented in nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp and nsCSSFrameConstructor.h, is responsible for creating the frame tree from the DOM tree. This process:\\n- Constructs frames based on CSS display properties\\n- Creates anonymous frames for special layout modes (flex, grid, tables)\\n- Maintains frame state across construction phases\\nThe nsFrameManager.cpp/h files manage the frame tree after construction, handling frame lifecycle and state transitions.\\n\\n**2. REFLOW PIPELINE (layout/generic/)**\\nThe reflow system is the core layout computation engine:\\n\\n**ReflowInput/ReflowOutput** (ReflowInput.cpp/h, ReflowOutput.cpp/h):\\n- ReflowInput contains all input parameters for a reflow operation (constraints, parent state, float information)\\n- ReflowOutput contains the computed metrics (size, overflow, baseline) returned from reflow\\n\\n**BlockReflowState** (BlockReflowState.cpp/h):\\n- Encapsulates state during block-level frame reflow\\n- Manages float handling and clear operations\\n- Tracks line breaking and margin collapsing\\n\\n**nsBlockFrame** (nsBlockFrame.cpp/h):\\n- Core implementation of block-level layout\\n- Handles reflow of block, inline, and float children\\n- Implements line breaking and text wrapping logic\\n- DoReflowInlineFrames and ReflowBlock are key methods\\n\\n**nsBlockReflowContext** (nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h):\\n- Context for reflowing individual block children\\n- Handles margin collapsing and positioning\\n\\n**nsLineLayout** (nsLineLayout.cpp/h) and **nsLineBox** (nsLineBox.cpp/h):\\n- Manage inline-level frame layout and line box creation\\n- Handle baseline alignment and text measurement\\n\\n**nsInlineFrame** (nsInlineFrame.cpp/h):\\n- Implements inline-level container layout\\n- Delegates to line layout for content arrangement\\n\\n**nsFloatManager** (nsFloatManager.cpp/h):\\n- Manages float positioning and clearing\\n- Maintains float regions for float avoidance calculations\\n- Essential for block layout's float handling\\n\\n**AbsoluteContainingBlock** (AbsoluteContainingBlock.cpp/h):\\n- Handles layout of absolutely and fixed-positioned children\\n- Computes absolute positioning constraints\\n\\n**nsPlaceholderFrame** (nsPlaceholderFrame.cpp/h):\\n- Placeholder for out-of-flow frames (floats, positioned elements)\\n- Links out-of-flow frames to their containing blocks\\n\\n**3. DIRTY FRAME INVALIDATION & FRAME STATE (layout/generic/)**\\nThe frame state system tracks which frames need reflow:\\n\\n**nsFrameStateBits.h**:\\n- Defines state bits used to mark frames as dirty\\n- NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY: Frame needs full reflow\\n- NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN: At least one child is dirty\\n- NS_FRAME_FIRST_REFLOW: Frame hasn't been reflowed yet\\n- NS_FRAME_IN_REFLOW: Frame is currently being reflowed\\n- NS_FRAME_REFLOW_ROOT: Frame can be a reflow root for dynamic reflows\\n\\n**nsFrameState.cpp/h**:\\n- Implementation of frame state bit management\\n- Methods to set, clear, and query state bits\\n\\n**nsIFrame.cpp/h**:\\n- Base frame interface with methods:\\n  - MarkSubtreeDirty(): Mark frame and descendants as dirty\\n  - IsSubtreeDirty(): Check if frame or descendants are dirty\\n  - ChildIsDirty(): Called when a child frame becomes dirty\\n  - DidReflow(): Clear dirty bits after reflow completion\\n  - InvalidateFrame(): Request visual invalidation\\n\\n**4. REFLOW ORCHESTRATION (layout/base/)**\\n**PresShell** (PresShell.cpp/h):\\n- Main entry point for reflow operations\\n- FrameNeedsReflow(): Mark frame dirty and schedule reflow\\n- Manages reflow batching and scheduling\\n- Coordinates with RestyleManager for style changes\\n\\n**nsPresContext** (nsPresContext.cpp/h):\\n- Presentation context containing reflow state\\n- Tracks reflow metrics and invalidated regions\\n\\n**nsRefreshDriver** (nsRefreshDriver.cpp/h):\\n- Coordinates screen update timing (vsync)\\n- Orchestrates style recalculation and reflow phases\\n- Manages reflow callbacks via nsIReflowCallback.h\\n\\n**5. HELPER COMPONENTS**\\n**ViewportFrame** (ViewportFrame.cpp/h) and **nsCanvasFrame** (nsCanvasFrame.cpp/h):\\n- Root frame types that manage the viewport and canvas\\n\\n**nsFrameList** (nsFrameList.cpp/h):\\n- Efficient doubly-linked list for frame management\\n\\nThe pipeline operates as follows:\\n1. Style changes trigger PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow(), which marks frames with dirty bits\\n2. nsRefreshDriver::Tick() initiates the reflow phase\\n3. PresShell::DoReflow() processes dirty frames from root to leaves\\n4. nsCSSFrameConstructor handles frame construction when needed\\n5. Block/inline layout engines (nsBlockFrame, nsLineLayout) compute positions/sizes\\n6. Float manager and absolute positioning handle special layout modes\\n7. Dirty bits are cleared after reflow completes in DidReflow()\\n8. Paint invalidation occurs for changed regions\\n\\nThis architecture enables efficient incremental layout updates by only reflowing dirty subtrees while maintaining layout correctness through careful frame state management.\"\n}\n",
